# Beta Agents Endpoints

</TagTitle>

<TagDescription slot="description">

(beta) Agents API

</TagDescription>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/agents \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_list\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_List agent entities._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Retrieve a list of agent entities sorted by creation time.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

##### type \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_list+responses+200+application-json+agent+completion_args+completionargs+response_format+responseformat+type\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/agents \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Create a agent that can be used within a conversation._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Create a new agent giving it instructions, tools, description. The agent is then available to be used as a regular assistant in a conversation or as part of an agent pool from which it can be used.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

##### type \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_create+request+completion_args+completionargs+response_format+responseformat+type\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/agents/\{agent\_id\} \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Retrieve an agent entity._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Given an agent retrieve an agent entity with its attributes.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### type \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_get+responses+200+application-json+completion_args+completionargs+response_format+responseformat+type\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>PATCH</b></Pill> /v1/agents/\{agent\_id\} \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Update an agent entity._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Update an agent attributes and create a new version.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

##### type \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update+request+completion_args+completionargs+response_format+responseformat+type\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

##### type \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update+responses+200+application-json+completion_args+completionargs+response_format+responseformat+type\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>PATCH</b></Pill> /v1/agents/\{agent\_id\}/version \{#operation-agents_api_v1_agents_update_version\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Update an agent version._

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

</OperationDescriptionSection>
